examples:[
"I am speaking on behalf of the company.",
"She accepted the award on behalf of her team.",
"He acted on behalf of his friend."
]
},
{
front: "emphasizes",
back: "เน้นย้ำ, ให้ความสำคัญกับบางสิ่ง",
level: "์nomal",
type: "verb",
category: "รายงาน",
examples: ["The teacher emphasizes the importance of practice.", "This study emphasizes the need for clean energy."],
synonyms: ["stress", "highlight", "underline"]
}
];

let allCards = DATA.slice(), cards = DATA.slice(), current = 0, flipped = false;
let currentLevel = 'all', currentType = 'all', currentCategory = 'all';

// Game mode state
let gameMode = 'off'; // 'off' | 'point' | 'dairy'
let points = 0;
let dairyGoal = 5;

function renderCard(){
  const cardEl = document.getElementById('card');
  cardEl.classList.remove('flipped');
  flipped = false;
  // when card is changed/rendered, close extend panel (same as pressing ปิด)
  closeExtend();
  // ensure extend button is hidden/disabled when rendering (card is unflipped)
  const extBtnInit = document.getElementById('extendBtn');
  if (extBtnInit) {
    extBtnInit.classList.add('hidden');
    extBtnInit.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    extBtnInit.disabled = true;
  }
  if(!cards || cards.length === 0){
    document.getElementById('front').innerHTML = 'ไม่มีการ์ด';
    document.getElementById('back').innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  const item = cards[current];
  document.getElementById('front').innerHTML = item.front;
  document.getElementById('back').innerHTML = '?';
}

function flipCard(){
  if(!cards || cards.length === 0) return;
  const cardEl = document.getElementById('card');
  const ext = document.getElementById('extendBtn'); // moved up for reuse
  if(!flipped){
    document.getElementById('back').innerHTML = cards[current].back;
    cardEl.classList.add('flipped'); flipped=true;
    // show and enable extend button only when back is visible
    if(ext){
      ext.classList.remove('hidden');
      ext.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
      ext.disabled = false;
    }
  } else {
    cardEl.classList.remove('flipped'); flipped=false;
    // hide and disable extend button when unflipping
    if(ext){
      ext.classList.add('hidden');
      ext.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
      ext.disabled = true;
    }
  }
  // when unflipping, ensure panel closed (if any)
  if(!flipped) closeExtend();
}

function nextCard(){ if(!cards || cards.length===0) return; current=(current+1)%cards.length; renderCard(); }
function prevCard(){ if(!cards || cards.length===0) return; current=(current-1+cards.length)%cards.length; renderCard(); }
function shuffleCards(){ if(!allCards) return; cards=cards.slice().sort(()=>Math.random()-0.5); current=0; renderCard(); renderCardList(); }
function speakCard(){ 
  if(!cards || cards.length===0) return;
  const u=new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(cards[current].front.replace(/<br>/g,' ')); 
  u.lang='en-US'; 
  speechSynthesis.speak(u); 
}

function renderCardList(){
  const list=document.getElementById('cardList'); list.innerHTML='';
  if(!cards) return;
  cards.forEach((c,i)=>{
    const li=document.createElement('li');
    li.innerHTML=c.front;
    li.onclick=()=>{current=i; renderCard();};
    list.appendChild(li);
  });
}

function toggleRight(){ document.getElementById('right-sidebar').classList.toggle('hidden'); }

// combined filters: level / type / category
function applyFilters(){
  cards = allCards.filter(c => {
    if(currentLevel !== 'all' && c.level !== currentLevel) return false;
    if(currentType !== 'all' && c.type !== currentType) return false;
    if(currentCategory !== 'all' && c.category !== currentCategory) return false;
    return true;
  });
  // keep current within range
  if(cards.length === 0) current = 0;
  else current = Math.min(current, cards.length - 1);
  renderCard();
  renderCardList();
}

function filterLevel(level, el){
  currentLevel = level;
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('#left-sidebar .level-btn');
  buttons.forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el) el.classList.add('active');
  applyFilters();
}

function filterType(type, el){
  currentType = type;
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('#left-sidebar .type-btn');
  buttons.forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el) el.classList.add('active');
  applyFilters();
}

function filterCategory(cat, el){
  currentCategory = cat;
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('#left-sidebar .category-btn');
  buttons.forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el) el.classList.add('active');
  applyFilters();
}

function setGameMode(mode, el){
  const dairyControls = document.getElementById('dairyControls');
  const correctSide = document.querySelector('.correct-side');
  const scoreOverlay = document.querySelector('.score-overlay');

  // toggle off if clicking the active mode again
  if(gameMode === mode){
    gameMode = 'off';
    document.querySelectorAll('#left-sidebar .game-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    // hide game UI
    if (correctSide) {
      correctSide.classList.add('hidden');
      correctSide.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
    }
    if (scoreOverlay) {
      scoreOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
      scoreOverlay.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
    }
    if (dairyControls) dairyControls.style.display = 'none';
    points = 0;
    updateScoreDisplay();
    return;
  }

  // enable selected mode
  gameMode = mode;
  document.querySelectorAll('#left-sidebar .game-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if(el) el.classList.add('active');

  // show game UI — animate only if it was hidden
  const wasHidden = correctSide ? correctSide.classList.contains('hidden') : true;

  if(wasHidden && correctSide && scoreOverlay){
    correctSide.classList.remove('hidden');
    correctSide.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    correctSide.classList.add('animate-in');

    scoreOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
    scoreOverlay.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    scoreOverlay.classList.add('animate-in');

    // cleanup animation class after it finishes
    correctSide.addEventListener('animationend', ()=> correctSide.classList.remove('animate-in'), { once: true });
    scoreOverlay.addEventListener('animationend', ()=> scoreOverlay.classList.remove('animate-in'), { once: true });
  } else {
    // already visible (switching modes) — just ensure visible without replaying animation
    if (correctSide) {
      correctSide.classList.remove('hidden');
      correctSide.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    }
    if (scoreOverlay) {
      scoreOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
      scoreOverlay.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    }
  }

  if(mode === 'dairy') {
    if (dairyControls) dairyControls.style.display = 'flex';
  } else {
    if (dairyControls) dairyControls.style.display = 'none';
  }

  points = 0;
  updateScoreDisplay();
}

function updateScoreDisplay(){
  const el = document.getElementById('scoreDisplay');
  if(gameMode === 'dairy'){
    el.textContent = points + ' / ' + dairyGoal;
  } else {
    el.textContent = String(points);
  }
}

// Called when user presses the Correct button
function handleCorrect(){
  if(!cards || cards.length === 0) return;
  if(gameMode === 'point'){
    points += 1;
  } else if(gameMode === 'dairy'){
    if(points < dairyGoal) points += 1;
  } else {
    // if mode off, just proceed
  }
  updateScoreDisplay();
  // short press animation on the correct button
  const btn = document.getElementById('correctBtn');
  if(btn){
    // add class, it will be removed after animationend
    btn.classList.add('btn-press');
    btn.addEventListener('animationend', ()=> btn.classList.remove('btn-press'), { once: true });
  }
  // move to next card
  nextCard();
}

document.addEventListener('keydown', e=>{
  if(e.code==='Space'){ e.preventDefault(); flipCard(); }
  if(e.code==='ArrowRight') nextCard();
  if(e.code==='ArrowLeft') prevCard();
  if(e.key.toLowerCase()==='s') shuffleCards();
  if(e.key.toLowerCase()==='p') speakCard();
});

// state used to remember whether correct-side was visible before opening extend
// let prevCorrectWasHidden = true;

function toggleExtend(e){
  // prevent flashcard click flip when pressing button
  if (e) e.stopPropagation();
  const panel = document.getElementById('extendPanel');
  if(panel.classList.contains('hidden')){
    openExtend();
  } else {
    closeExtend();
  }
}

function openExtend(){
  const panel = document.getElementById('extendPanel');
  // populate and show panel
  populateExtendPanel();
  panel.classList.remove('hidden');
  panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
  // add entrance animation if desired
  panel.classList.add('animate-in');
  panel.addEventListener('animationend', ()=> panel.classList.remove('animate-in'), { once: true });
  // keep the correct-side (ถูก) visible while extend panel is open
}

function closeExtend(){
  const panel = document.getElementById('extendPanel');

  panel.classList.add('hidden');
  panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
  // restore the left "ถูก" button when closing extend if a game mode is active
  const correctSide = document.querySelector('.correct-side');
  if (correctSide && gameMode !== 'off') {
    correctSide.classList.remove('hidden');
    correctSide.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
    // play a light pop animation when restoring (matches other UI)
    correctSide.classList.add('animate-in');
    correctSide.addEventListener('animationend', () => correctSide.classList.remove('animate-in'), { once: true });
  }
}

function populateExtendPanel(){
  const panel = document.getElementById('extendPanel');
  const header = document.getElementById('extendHeader');
  const content = document.getElementById('extendContent');
  if(!cards || cards.length === 0){
    header.innerText = 'ไม่มีคำ';
    content.innerHTML = '<div>ไม่มีข้อมูล</div>';
    return;
  }
  const item = cards[current];
  // header larger: english word
  header.innerText = item.front || 'ไม่มีคำ';

  // --- parse back/thai and extract inline "Synonyms: ..." if present ---
  const backRaw = item.back ? String(item.back) : '';
  // Normalize <br> to newline for easier parsing
  const backNormalized = backRaw.replace(/<br\s*\/?>/gi, '\n');
  let thai = backRaw; // default display (keeps original HTML if no change)
  let synonymsFromBack = [];

  // Look for "Synonyms: ..." (case-insensitive) at end or on its own line
  const synMatch = backNormalized.match(/(?:^|\n)\s*Synonyms:\s*(.+?)(?:\n|$)/i);
  if (synMatch) {
    const synStr = synMatch[1].trim();
    if (synStr) {
      synonymsFromBack = synStr.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    }
    // remove the Synonyms: line from thai and restore <br> for display
    thai = backNormalized.replace(/(?:\n\s*Synonyms:\s*.+?)(?:\n|$)/i, '').replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
  } else {
    // no inline synonyms found — keep original back HTML
    thai = backRaw;
  }

  // build other fields
  const typeText = item.type ? item.type : 'ไม่ระบุประเภทคำ';
  const level = item.level ? item.level : '-';
  const examples = Array.isArray(item.examples) ? item.examples : (typeof item.example === 'string' ? [item.example] : []);

  // collect synonyms: accept item.synonyms (array or string) and include parsed ones
  let synonyms = [];
  if (Array.isArray(item.synonyms)) {
    synonyms = item.synonyms.map(s => String(s).trim()).filter(Boolean);
  } else if (typeof item.synonyms === 'string' && item.synonyms.trim()) {
    synonyms = item.synonyms.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  }
  // append parsed synonyms from backNormalized, avoid duplicates
  synonymsFromBack.forEach(s => { if (s && !synonyms.includes(s)) synonyms.push(s); });

  // create HTML
  let html = '';
  html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:8px;">ชนิดคำ</div>';
  html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: ชนิดคำ -->';
  html += `<div style="margin-bottom:8px;">${escapeHtml(typeText)}</div>`;

  html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:6px;">คำแปลภาษาไทย</div>';
  html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: คำแปลภาษาไทย -->';
  // thai may contain <br> for formatting; insert as raw HTML
  html += `<div style="margin-bottom:8px;">${thai}</div>`;

  // render synonyms as its own heading when present
  if (synonyms.length > 0) {
    html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:6px;">คำพ้องความหมาย</div>';
    html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: Synonyms -->';
    html += `<div style="margin-bottom:8px;">${escapeHtml(synonyms.join(', '))}</div>`;
  }

  html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:6px;">ระดับความยาก</div>';
  html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: ระดับความยาก -->';
  html += `<div style="margin-bottom:8px;">${level}</div>`;

  html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:6px;">ตัวอย่าง</div>';
  html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: ตัวอย่าง -->';
  if (examples.length === 0) {
    html += '<div>ไม่มีตัวอย่าง</div>';
  } else {
    html += '<ul style="margin:6px 0 12px 18px;">';
    examples.forEach(ex => { html += `<li style="margin-bottom:6px;">${escapeHtml(ex)}</li>`; });
    html += '</ul>';
  }

  // image (optional)
  const imageUrl = (item.image && typeof item.image === 'string' && item.image.trim()) ? item.image.trim() : null;
  if (imageUrl) {
    html += '<div style="font-weight:800; color:var(--accent); margin-top:6px;">รูปภาพ</div>';
    html += '<!-- ใส่ข้อมูล: รูปภาพ -->';
    html += `<img src="${escapeHtml(imageUrl)}" alt="${escapeHtml(item.front || '')}">`;
  }

  content.innerHTML = html;
  // make content scroll to top
  content.scrollTop = 0;
}

// small helper to sanitize simple text/HTML in data
function escapeHtml(str){
  if(str == null) return '';
  return String(str).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;');
}

// Ensure extend panel hidden on init and extend button disabled
const _extendPanel = document.getElementById('extendPanel');
if (_extendPanel) {
  _extendPanel.classList.add('hidden');
  _extendPanel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
}
const _initExt = document.getElementById('extendBtn');
if (_initExt) {
  _initExt.classList.add('hidden');
  _initExt.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  _initExt.disabled = true;
}

// Init app UI state (clean, non-duplicated)
applyFilters();
renderCardList(); // populate right list

// clear game mode buttons active state
const mp = document.getElementById('modePointBtn');
const md = document.getElementById('modeDairyBtn');
if (mp) mp.classList.remove('active');
if (md) md.classList.remove('active');

// ensure game UI hidden at start
const cs = document.querySelector('.correct-side');
const so = document.querySelector('.score-overlay');
if (cs) cs.classList.add('hidden');
if (so) so.classList.add('hidden');

// hide dairy controls initially
const dc = document.getElementById('dairyControls');
if (dc) dc.style.display = 'none';

// ensure score shown correctly
updateScoreDisplay();
